	<script type="text/javascript">

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};
	</script>

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};
	</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};
	</script>

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};

	<script type="text/javascript">

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};
	</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};
	</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">

	wfb_ChangeTable = function(number, liga)
	{
		active_table = '.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tabelle_' + number;
		active_tab = '.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_' + number;

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').fadeToggle(400);
		$(active_table).delay(400).fadeToggle(400);

		$('.scrollable_tables[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .active').removeClass("active");
		$(active_table).addClass("active");

		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] .tab').removeClass("active");
		$(active_tab).addClass("active");
	};

	wfb_TablesInit = function()
	{
		$('.scrollable_tabs[data-liga="' + liga + '"] #tab_0').addClass("active");
	};
	</script>
